<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">每场冒险世界一次，</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当一次攻击或者一个效果会导致</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">牧群</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">死亡，本能力会将这次攻击完全无视，同时连带这次攻击附带的其他效果也会被一并无视。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">若该次攻击或者效果为范围能力或者复数目标，则本能力只会使其作用在</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">牧群</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">身上的效果无效，并不会影响其他目标。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意：本能力带来的效果是无视，所以哪怕不可避免的伤害，本能力依然可以对其生效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：浮士德，本名萨沙，整合运动干部，梅菲斯特的挚友，剧情开始是和梅菲斯特一起抵抗龙门近卫局和罗德岛的进攻，最后为了保护梅菲斯特和幻影弩手小队让其撤退，战死在龙门。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">珍视部下，性格沉稳，能够顾全大局。常常与梅菲斯特一同出现。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">与梅菲斯特自小相识，互相信任帮助。经常在其因愤怒失去理智下达错误的指令时进行劝导挽回。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">有着深青绿色有些凌乱的短发，尖耳朵，皮肤有些泛青灰色。深绿色的眼睛，红黑色的蛇瞳，眼下有几片蛇鳞。肩上披着黑色外套，右臂上套着整合运动指挥官的橙色袖标（位置与梅菲斯特相对）。穿着白色的宽松裤子，黑色的短靴，手持特殊改装过的弩。本强化改造后浮士德为牧群版本浮士德，与原版有出入。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">他具备如下属性：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生理系属性：力量</font><font face="宋体">4  敏捷16  耐力6</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体"> </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p></td></tr></table>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt 9pt 0pt 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">专长：闪避格挡</font><font face="宋体">2，轻灵战士2，钢铁意志2，警觉1</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体积：</font><font face="宋体">5（中型生物）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">刻度：源石技力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">防御：</font><font face="宋体">12/12的轻甲，具有【防弹】【防能量武器】【魔法】特性</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">武器：武器伤害</font><font face="宋体">8L，破甲12，具备【8加骰】【魔法】【超级贯穿】特性的弩</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">自律行动：浮士德拥有独立的先攻和自己的回合，轮到浮士德行动时，你可以如同控制自己行动一般控制浮士德行动。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">幻影弩手：浮士德的远程枪械攻击检定获得</font><font face="宋体">12DP内在加值；浮士德可以以迅捷动作支付5点源石技力进入隐身状态，持续至多一小时，这是一个B级别的特异本质的反侦测能力，浮士德在发动此隐身能力时可以额外支付X点源石技力，使自身触及距离内X名单位同样进入隐身状态，X的数值没有上限（注意，在进行侦测与定位对抗时，使用浮士德的对应数据进行对抗）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">致命射击：浮士德每次进行远程枪械攻击时会进行充能，每当充能次数达到两层时，浮士德下一次进行远程枪械攻击时会消耗全部的充能次数和全部的源石技力刻度，使此次远程枪械攻击额外造成所消耗的源石技力刻度</font><font face="宋体">*1点力场严重伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：瞄准，射击。。。。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：被动</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-AUTOSPACE: ideograph-numeric; mso-pagination: none"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：浮士德立即获得源石技艺通用技能树下等级为</font><font face="宋体">B级以下的1个技艺（或者3个C级技艺，或者9个D级技艺）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(255,0,0); LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
